</div></div><div class="content"><div class="formulation clearfix"><h4 class="accesshide">Question text</h4><input type="hidden" name="q747714:49_:sequencecheck" value="3" /><div class="qtext"><p dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;">Which language does the regular expression a+b* describe?</p></div><fieldset class="ablock no-overflow visual-scroll-x"><legend class="prompt h6 font-weight-normal sr-only"><span class="sr-only">Question 49</span> Select one:</legend><div class="answer"><div class="r0 correct"><input type="radio" name="q747714:49_answer" disabled="disabled" value="0" id="q747714:49_answer0" aria-labelledby="q747714:49_answer0_label" checked="checked" /><div class="d-flex w-auto" id="q747714:49_answer0_label" data-region="answer-label"><span class="answernumber">a. </span><div class="flex-fill ml-1"><p dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;">All strings that start with n&gt;0 a's followed by m&gt;=0 b's, where m and n are integers.</p></div></div> <span class="ml-1"><i class="icon fa fa-check text-success fa-fw "  title="Correct" role="img" aria-label="Correct"></i></span></div>
<div class="r1"><input type="radio" name="q747714:49_answer" disabled="disabled" value="1" id="q747714:49_answer1" aria-labelledby="q747714:49_answer1_label" /><div class="d-flex w-auto" id="q747714:49_answer1_label" data-region="answer-label"><span class="answernumber">b. </span><div class="flex-fill ml-1"><p dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;">All strings of a's and b's that start with at least one a.&nbsp;<br></p></div></div> </div>
<div class="r0"><input type="radio" name="q747714:49_answer" disabled="disabled" value="2" id="q747714:49_answer2" aria-labelledby="q747714:49_answer2_label" /><div class="d-flex w-auto" id="q747714:49_answer2_label" data-region="answer-label"><span class="answernumber">c. </span><div class="flex-fill ml-1"><p dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;">All strings starting with a's followed by b's.</p></div></div> </div>
<div class="r1"><input type="radio" name="q747714:49_answer" disabled="disabled" value="3" id="q747714:49_answer3" aria-labelledby="q747714:49_answer3_label" /><div class="d-flex w-auto" id="q747714:49_answer3_label" data-region="answer-label"><span class="answernumber">d. </span><div class="flex-fill ml-1"><p dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;">All strings consisting of an arbitrary number (including zero) of triples a+b , for example, a+b , a+ba+b , a+ba+ba+b, etc.&nbsp;</p></div></div> </div>
<div class="r0"><input type="radio" name="q747714:49_answer" disabled="disabled" value="4" id="q747714:49_answer4" aria-labelledby="q747714:49_answer4_label" /><div class="d-flex w-auto" id="q747714:49_answer4_label" data-region="answer-label"><span class="answernumber">e. </span><div class="flex-fill ml-1"><p dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;">All strings of a's and b's that have at least one a.&nbsp;</p></div></div> </div>

</span>
                            </button>
                        </div>
                    </div>
